endless cycle of evenings and the violent heat of the summer. it took us a very long time to get right, from an aching piano demo to where is it now. it’s close to my heart. i hope you like This line I remember writing down when I was standing on my porch watching my friends fiddle with the speakers inside and thinking \&quot;oh, in about ten seconds they&#39;re gonna go...\&quot; I wrote this lyric in November of 2016, but then in December me and my friend drank a bunch of 1 part champagne, 1 part vodka cocktails which we christened Suicides and DJ-ed a really raucous Christmas party - we had this crazy room going then blew the speakers spectacularly and ghosted out of there. So yeah. Kind of about me.       <div class="annotation_label">
        
          <h3 class="u-inline">
            About “Perfect Places”
          </h3>
        
        
      </div>
      <div class="rich_text_formatting">
        <p>“Perfect Places” concerns a narrative often present at teenage parties, a story of drug usage and sex. Lorde ends the song and the album in general with a groundbreaking message: the mentalities and experiences involved with these practices are not actually so perfect, even though they may feel euphoric. The late teenage years are, above anything, imperfect.</p>

<p>The track was released as a promotional single from <em>Melodrama</em>, Lorde’s sophomore album. <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Jack-antonoff" rel="noopener" data-api_path="/artists/264329">Jack Antonoff</a> provided a hand in the background vocals and production of the song, much like the rest of <em>Melodrama</em>.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="song_metadata u-xx_large_bottom_margin"></div>
    </div>

    <div class="column_layout-column_span-initial_content">
      <div initial-content-for="question_list">
  <ul>
    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">What have the artists said about the song?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="verified_answer">
    <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Lorde">
      <div
        class="verified_answer-artist_avatar user_avatar user_avatar--x_large clipped_background_image clipped_background_image--background_fill"
        style="background-image: url('https://images.genius.com/a2fd0bb1affd9235323dfed76a982644.393x393x1.png')"
      ></div>
    </a>

    <div class="verified_answer-main">
      <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Lorde" class="text_label verified_answer-artist">Lorde:</a>

      <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
        <p>this is a special one. i was living in new york during summer last year, writing melodrama – i’d ride across the brooklyn bridge every day, or sit on the subway uptown in the heat, then go back home to new zealand winter for a week at a time to party with my friends. my life was like a weird little etch-a-sketch i kept scribbling on and resetting. and all last summer, i couldn’t shake the feeling that everyone i knew or saw was searching for something – trying to transcend the news and the screaming pavements, drinking that one drink hoping it’d get them someplace higher. this song comes from that endless cycle of evenings and the violent heat of the summer. it took us a very long time to get right, from an aching piano demo to where is it now. it’s close to my heart. i hope you like it.</p>
      </div>

      
        <div class="verified_answer-attribution">
          <a href="https://www.facebook.com/lordemusic/photos/a.547295165288208.125876.508598672491191/1686918854659161/?type=3" class="text_label text_label--button text_label--purple" target="_blank">via Facebook</a>
        </div>
      
    </div>
  </div>


</li>

    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">Are there any translations for this song?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
    <p>Yes!</p>

</ul>
  </div>


</li>

    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">What has Lorde said about the writing process of this song?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
    <p>Lorde revealed to <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2017/04/12/magazine/the-return-of-lorde.html" rel="noopener nofollow"><i>The New York Times</i></a> that this track was difficult to complete.</p>

<blockquote><p>It’s lived a million lives. We’ve tried it at different tempos, used different voicings, took it half time, made it weird and druggy, but that didn’t work. A big problem is that there’s so much to the song. The other day I had a breakthrough: What if we delete the entire prechorus? Just take it out, and I never have to hear it again in my life? We did, and now the whole thing follows a much simpler trajectory.</p></blockquote>
  </div>


</li>

    
    
  </ul>
</div>
